American Construction of Large Airships Views Japan as a Formidable Enemy

Former Air Force Commander Mitchell Suggests Fifty Airships Could Flatten the Three Islands 24

(Washington) Former U.S. Army Air Service Chief Major General Mitchell today suggested to the Federal Aviation Commission that Japan is America's most dangerous enemy. Therefore, the aviation development of the U.S. Army and Navy must keep this point firmly in mind. The Aviation Commission is currently conducting an investigation of Army and Navy aviation. Mitchell suggested immediately building a large fleet of combat airships and refuted the argument that airships are not suitable for war. As for the repeated accidents involving airships, they are due to improper piloting. He believes that with fifty airships, Japan could be attacked and the three islands flattened within two days. If the navy were used, it would take a long time. Japan is "our most dangerous enemy," so the air force policy of the United States should also be shifted accordingly. "When we design and build airplanes, we must aim to build airplanes that can attack Japan, just as British airplanes are used to attack Europe." Mitchell also offered his expertise for government reference. He believes that the airplanes he advocates should have a flying range of six thousand miles and considers the existing bombers of the U.S. Army to be useless because bombers must be able to ascend to over 35,000 feet to hide in the clouds and avoid being spotted by the enemy. Mitchell believes that the Akron airship disaster two years ago was extremely shameful and vehemently criticized the current policy of the Navy Department of transferring the commanders of the Navy and Air Force to each other. He believes that the airship pilots should be experts, and if naval personnel take over, it is tantamount to fighting without training. Mitchell has always advocated that the Air Force should have a dedicated department and said that modern warfare depends entirely on airplanes, so the expansion of the U.S. Air Force should not lag far behind other countries. (National News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

U.S. Army Air Corps Converted to Independent Organization

Nine Hundred Airplanes Ready to Mobilize at Any Time 25

(Washington) The War Department announced today that the newly formed air corps of the General Headquarters will establish an independent air force so that it can operate independently from the army. According to the official announcement, 900 airplanes will be able to undertake offensive or defensive missions upon receiving mobilization orders. According to the plan announced today, all army flying corps fighters will be organized into the air force of the General Headquarters, concentrated at army airfields from California to near Virginia. The General Headquarters will be located at Langley Field, which is located across the Potomac River from Washington. The General Headquarters Air Force will report directly to the General Staff, rather than the Army Air Corps. The status of the Army Air Corps has been weakened as a result, and the power of Major General Foulois, the director of the Air Corps, has also been greatly reduced. A congressional investigating committee requested Foulois's dismissal several weeks ago. (National News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Japanese Naval Representative Talks About Mission to England

Preparing to Formally Announce the Abolition of the Treaty and Unilaterally Seek Understanding from Britain and America 27

Japanese Navy Rear Admiral Yamamoto, on his way to England, revealed this news. Today, he told a news interviewer that the mission of this trip is to announce the abolition of the current naval treaty and to present a new plan for world peace based on reducing offensive armaments. He said that if Britain and America understand Japan's true reasons for abolishing the treaty, any disturbances that may occur in Japan's relations with Britain and America will be extinguished early. Japan firmly believes that the ratios established in the Washington Naval Treaty were based on the military strength of the three signatory countries at the time, not on the self-defense needs of the three countries. This is one of the reasons for Japan's abolition of the treaty. Japan believes that countries should be allowed to have weapons sufficient to guarantee national security, and countries should not have armaments sufficient to endanger other countries. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

Rear Admiral Yamamoto Isoroku, the Japanese government's disarmament representative in Seattle, and his party arrived in Seattle on the morning of the 2nd. Yamamoto replied that the Japanese are always concerned about the actions of the U.S. Combined Fleet, but this is not nervous. The Combined Fleet's exercise in Alaska is the natural right of the British Navy, and Japan does not want to interfere. (Japanese United News dispatch, 2nd)

Japanese Army's Interference in Internal Affairs

(Tokyo) The government is quite perplexed about the army's booklet issue, and its feelings are as follows: Prime Minister Okada often discusses national defense issues with the Minister of the Army, and their opinions are completely consistent. As for general national policies, if the content of the booklet is the ambition of the entire army, then Minister of the Army Hayashi should have advised the Prime Minister before publishing it, or advocated it in the cabinet meeting. If it is a personal view, it should be discussed separately. Now, it is published as an official document, which is a bit rash. Social policies, economic policies, rural policies, etc., are all decided by the cabinet meeting, and each responsible province is responsible for implementing them. Now, the army directly criticizes them, which is very inappropriate. The Prime Minister will wait for Minister of the Army Hayashi to return to Tokyo to question his beliefs. (Dentsu dispatch, 3rd)

(Dentsu dispatch, 3rd)

(Tokyo) At 3:00 p.m. today, the Seiyukai held a general affairs meeting at its headquarters to discuss the issue of the booklet published by the army. The result was a consensus as follows: (1) Although the booklet expresses the modern meaning of national defense very well, it is difficult to sympathize with the reform of the current economic system, which all returns to the unified state control. (2) If it is an important opinion, it should be consulted with the cabinet meeting first, and then it can be published. This time, it was published independently, which is a bit rash. Does Prime Minister Okada have any sense of responsibility for this? (3) During the budget preparation period, and when preparing to convene a temporary parliament, the army suddenly published a booklet. What is its true intention? In short, the army's interference outside of its jurisdiction and its sense of oppression of other institutions are very regrettable. (Dentsu dispatch, 3rd)

British Monetary Policy Maintains the Independent Status of the Gold Pound 42

Foreign Secretary Chamberlain Indicates No Intention to Participate in International Conference 43

(London) Foreign Secretary Chamberlain stated today that Britain has no intention of participating in any international exchange rate stabilization conference for the time being. Chamberlain spoke at a banking banquet tonight, saying that he would like to reiterate the British government's policy, namely that the government will maintain the independent status of the pound sterling and the Exchange Equalisation Account. The establishment of the Exchange Equalisation Account is to avoid excessive fluctuations in exchange rates. Chamberlain added, "I feel that we are gradually tired of international conferences, because conferences require the smoothest atmosphere, but this kind of atmosphere is not always available, so I think that for the time being, we should first have private discussions." Chamberlain's remarks were probably due to recent news from New York, saying that bankers there believe that Britain will lower the pound sterling and restore it to its old parity with the U.S. dollar. At that time, the exchange rate can be stabilized. (National News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(London) Financial Secretary Chamberlain said today before a group of bankers and merchants in the City of London that the first eight of this year increased by 20 million gold pounds, but the difficulties of international trade seem to be increasing. The price of the pound has weakened slightly recently due to seasonal factors, and it has become more severe due to foreign financial and political incidents. He believes that this cannot be regarded as a scene of the past. The government's current policy is to maintain the independence of the pound sterling and prevent excessive fluctuations. The government has never sought to set the exchange rate at a certain point, or sought to maintain its price within a certain limit, to fight against seasonal and other powerful forces. The connections between the various states inside and outside the empire and the pound sterling have been safely maintained, and it is gradually recognized as a feature of the international monetary system. The Financial Secretary then praised the steps taken to establish central banks within the empire last year, saying that this is enough to promote their common imperial goal of monetary policy. The Financial Secretary then presented statistics to prove the progress of trade and production. Compared with the same quarter of last year, the index in the second quarter of this year has increased as follows:

April to June of this year Same quarter last year

Textiles 91 86

Chemicals 109 101

Machinery and shipbuilding 119 97

Copper and iron 104 78

The Financial Secretary said that the ships currently under construction have doubled compared to before, and the number of ships lying idle has been reduced by half. Retail sales in August increased by 5% compared to the same month last year, which proves that the progress of industry has gradually had a good impact on the purchasing power of the people. The Financial Secretary concluded that the ironclad evidence of the progress of trade is greater than that expressed by the number of unemployed people. Former Financial Secretary Horne is now a giant in the British business community. It is said that he believes that the value of the pound sterling has recently been too high. If we can return it to another price, it can benefit British bankers. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Fluctuations in Japanese Yen Exchange Rate; Japan Does Not Wish To Take Action 44

(Tokyo) Mr. Fukai, the Governor of the Bank of Japan, told reporters today that the Bank of Japan does not wish to take any action to curb fluctuations in the yen exchange rate. Rumors that the Bank of Japan intends to work with the Ministry of Finance and the Yokohama Specie Bank to manage foreign trade to prevent the yen from continuing to fall are unfounded. The yen is valued against the US dollar in past decades but has switched to being valued against the pound sterling since March of last year. Under the current circumstances, it is best to convert to the pound sterling. There are indeed fluctuations in the price of gold in the foreign gold market and the buying price, but Japan has not yet made any decision on whether to increase the buying price. (Reuters dispatch of the 3rd)

Germans Commemorate Hindenburg's Achievements 45

General Tower in Tannenberg Open to the Public; People Flock to Pay Respects 46

(Berlin) Today is the birthday of the late President Hindenburg. Had he lived, he would have been eighty-seven years old today. Although Mr. Hindenburg is dead, the entire German nation still commemorates his great achievements. All newspapers today contain records commemorating the late President. A grand commemorative ceremony was held in Tannenberg. Führer Hitler also instructed the organization of a special honor guard to stand in front of Hindenburg's tomb in Tannenberg, and the people who went to Hindenburg's tomb to pay their respects are increasing. The General Tower in Tannenberg, where Mr. Hindenburg is buried, has been reopened today. Many dignitaries went to present wreaths, including Führer Hitler. The interior of the Tannenberg Memorial Hall will be renovated this winter. How Hindenburg's tomb will be completed, and its style, have also been submitted to Mr. Hitler for his decision. After the General Tower is redecorated, busts of the generals who participated in the Battle of Tannenberg will be displayed inside. The remaining two towers, such as "Vanguard Soldiers" and "East Prussia," will also be transformed to make them even more magnificent. (National Telegram of the 2nd)

League of Nations Should Not Interfere in the Chaco Dispute; US State Department Issues Statement 47

(Washington) Assistant Secretary of State Welles issued a statement saying that the League of Nations has no qualifications to arbitrate the South American Chaco dispute and is an outsider. The chairman of the Council of the League of Nations is Czech Foreign Minister Beneš, "and Mr. Beneš knows nothing about Latin American issues." Moreover, Bolivia and Paraguay have already accepted the proposal of Argentine Foreign Minister Saavedra, and it is regrettable that the League of Nations has interfered at this time. (Note: The United States and Argentina had proposed to Bolivia and Paraguay: (1) Both sides should cease fire immediately; (2) Each side should send plenipotentiary representatives to choose a place to meet and discuss peace terms. (Havas dispatch of the 2nd)

The Yellow River is Rising Again 52

(Jinan) According to a telegram from the hydrological station in Shaan County to the River Bureau, the river water rose a total of 2.73 meters from the morning of the 1st to the 3rd, with a water level of 295.06 meters, only 4 centimeters lower than the highest water level of the great flood this year. The flow rate has also increased to 9,900 cubic meters per second. All sections within the province are also rising. Luokou rose by 1 inch, with a water level of 29.41 meters. The River Bureau has telegraphed to the entire river again to strictly prevent floods. (Special dispatch of the 3rd)

(Kaifeng) On the morning of the 3rd, Xiainan rose by 5 inches, Shangnan rose by 6.4 inches, Shangbei rose by 5 inches, and Dongqin rose by 3.7 inches. Chen Ruzhen, Director of the River Bureau, went up the river from Liuyuankou to Guangwu, and Section Chief Wu went to Xibatou to supervise the construction of drainage ditches for protection. (Special dispatch of the 3rd)

The head dam of the remaining twenty forts eroded by five zhang and five chi, and the Second Dam eroded by seven zhang. More than 800 disaster victims from Fugou County gathered in Bianbei to request relief. (Special dispatch of the 3rd)

Page 9

The Ninth Congress of the Far Eastern Association of Tropical Medicine Opened in Nanjing Yesterday

More Than Three Hundred Delegates from Various Countries Visit the Mausoleum in the Morning and Then Elect Directors 94

The Ninth Far Eastern Association of Tropical Medicine opened yesterday, with more than three hundred delegates from various countries attending. At 8 a.m., led by Liu Jui-heng, they traveled by car to visit the mausoleum and presented wreaths, singing the party song together. Despite the heavy rain, the order was very solemn. They then returned to the Lichi Society to elect directors. A total of more than fifty directors were elected from various countries. Afterwards, the first board meeting was held at the Ministry of Health, discussing association affairs. After lunch, the opening ceremony of the general meeting was held at 2 p.m. in the auditorium of the Lichi Society. Important government officials such as President Wang, Huang Shao-hong, Wang Shih-chieh, Zou Lin, Fu Ju-lin, Shih Ying, and Chu Min-yi all attended. Foreign guests included Suma, the Japanese Consul General in Beijing, and Rong Ji, Counselor of the German Embassy. Chairman Liu Jui-heng first read Chairman Lin's congratulatory message, followed by President Wang's speech, translated by Zhang Ping-qun. Huang Shao-hong then gave a speech, translated by Huang Ren-lin. Shih Ying then delivered a speech in English, and finally, Chairman Liu Jui-heng gave the opening address and read out congratulatory telegrams from various places. The meeting adjourned for a photo at 3 p.m. At 8 p.m., Wang hosted a banquet for the delegates at the Mingzhi Building of the Examination Yuan. The guests and hosts dispersed happily at 9:30 p.m. The conference is scheduled to continue at 9 a.m. this morning at the Ministry of Health to read papers, divided into four groups: (1) Internal Medicine, (2) Pathology, (3) Surgery, Obstetrics, Optics, Ophthalmology, and Dentistry, and (4) Plague and Cholera, etc., to be held separately. A total of thirty-two papers will be presented, and it is said that they all have great value in medicine. The various circumstances of the opening of this conference are recorded separately as follows:

▲ Establishment History　Around 1908 (three years before the founding of the Republic of China), medical experts from various Eastern countries, realizing that world transportation was becoming increasingly convenient and that various diseases had become internationalized, no longer suitable for closed-door research, jointly planned to organize an international medical organization to hold regular meetings for mutual discussion. Thus, the Far Eastern Association of Tropical Medicine was established. Since then, eight conferences have been held, with the dates and locations as follows: First Session, Manila, 1910; Second Session, Hong Kong, 1912; Third Session, Annam, 1913; Fourth Session, Java, 1921; Fifth Session, Singapore, 1923; Sixth Session, Tokyo, Japan, 1925; Seventh Session, India, 1927; Eighth Session, Siam, 1930. The member countries are: 1. Australia, 2. India and its dependencies, 3. China, 4. Federated Malay States, 5. Philippines, 6. Hong Kong, 7. Annam, 8. Japan, 9. Honolulu, 10. Straits Settlements, 11. Dutch East Indies, 12. Siam, 13. United States, 14. Macau. At the Eighth Conference in Siam in 1930, the former Ministry of Health of our country officially notified and invited the next conference to be held in China in 1933. The conference passed the motion, but due to the national crisis, it could not be held as scheduled. After notifying the member countries, it was changed to be held in Beijing from October 1st to 7th this year. This is a general overview of the past history of this conference.

▲ Preparations　The conference period was originally scheduled for October 1st to 7th, but now, because the ships carrying delegates from various countries to Shanghai arrive around the 1st and 2nd, the official opening will be changed to the 3rd, with only registration and other procedures on the 2nd. President Wang Jingwei of the Executive Yuan has been invited to serve as honorary president of the conference, and Vice President Kong Xiangxi and Minister of Interior Huang Shao-hong have been appointed as honorary vice presidents of the conference. Director Liu Jui-heng of the Ministry of Health is the acting president of the conference, and medical celebrities Wu Lien-teh, Niu Hui-sheng, and Chu Min-yi have been appointed as honorary advisors to the conference. The names of the executive committee secretary, vice presidents and secretaries of various districts are as follows: Executive Committee Secretary Jin Bao-shan, North China District, Vice President Fang Qing, Secretary Li Zong-en, Central China District, Vice President Yan Fu-qing, Secretary Zhu Heng-bi, South China District, Vice President Li Shu-fen, Secretary Chen Yi-ping. In addition, (1) a Paper Committee has been established, with Wu Lien-teh and Lin Zong-yang as members, responsible for organizing, arranging, printing papers, etc. (2) A Arrangement Committee has been established, with Zhu Zhang-guang and Guo Cheng-zhi as members, responsible for arranging the conference venue and scientific exhibition, etc. (3) An Reception Committee has been established, with Huang Ren-lin, Qi Shou-nan, and Jiang Li-geng-sheng as members, responsible for all reception matters during the conference. (4) A Transportation Committee has been established, with Shen Ke-fei and Chen Xiang-tao as members, responsible for coordinating the transportation of members to and from the conference. The conference venue is located at the Lichi Society on Huangpu Road, and the group meetings will be held at the Ministry of Health. After the conference, groups will tour Beijing, Hangzhou, and other places, and reception committees will be organized in Beijing and Shanghai to handle reception matters upon the arrival of members from various countries. The accommodations for members in Beijing will be in the newly completed dormitories of the Central Hospital, and those with families will stay in hotels. It is estimated that approximately 270 to 280 delegates and members from various countries will attend. Over 170 papers have been received, all of which are valuable works from experts in various countries. After the conference, they will be compiled into a volume and distributed to relevant medical institutions and organizations at home and abroad. In addition, in order to promote our country's health facilities in recent years, a summary report on the actual situation of central and local health work has been compiled and printed into a booklet for distribution to members from various countries, so as to enhance their understanding of our country's health facilities in recent years and to assist in external promotion.

▲ Chairman Lin's Congratulatory Message "The world evolves, the universe communicates, medicine prospers, and specialization is valued. This conference is the beginning of the Far East, promoting benevolence, with excellent reputation. With broad vision and nurturing, nature creates wonders. All beings with blood and breath share the same physiology. Health, peace, early death, who can fathom the heavens? Human determination surpasses the heavens, and science succeeds. Distinguished scholars, compassionate at heart, humbly discuss, resolving doubts. Deep thought and experimentation, awaken the ignorant. Like a star that illuminates, like the sun at its zenith. Miraculous prescriptions and unique skills, infinitely subtle. With one heart to save the world, with complete impartiality."

▲ President Wang's Speech "Distinguished Delegates and Members, as the honorary president of this conference, I am honored to extend a welcome to the representatives and members from various friendly nations present here today. At the Eighth Conference of your Association in Siam in 1930, the government of our country sent a telegram inviting the Ninth Conference to be held in Nanjing, the capital of our country, which was approved. It was originally scheduled to be held as scheduled in October of last year, but due to the situation in the Far East, it was postponed for one year. Today, representatives and members from India, Hong Kong, Annam, Japan, Macau, the Dutch East Indies, Siam, the Federated Malay States, the Straits Settlements, the Philippines, the United States, and the International Federation have come from afar as scheduled. Scientists from all over the world gather together with a spirit of mutual love to discuss the diseases, sufferings, and medical relief methods of mankind, which is a very important and great undertaking. Our country feels exceptionally honored. Today, most of the countries participating in the meeting are affected by tropical diseases, and they are equally concerned about the prevention and treatment of tropical diseases. The common purpose of the participating countries has united them to seek happiness for mankind. The eastward transmission of Western science has been going on for only over three hundred years in history, while the introduction of modern medicine into our country has only been going on for decades. Since the establishment of the National Government, special attention has been paid to the construction of health undertakings, and efforts have been made to develop and promote them. At present, various central and local health, medical, and epidemic prevention agencies have been established one after another and are actively carrying out their work. The gentlemen present here today are all the backbone of the medical and health administration circles in the Far East. We all know that this is the first time that your association has held a meeting in our country. This will be permanently recorded in the history of science and in the history of our country. I sincerely hope that while exchanging research experiences, you will visit the medical and health construction in various parts of our country. Our country welcomes you very much, and at the same time hopes to obtain your valuable advice. I now extend my sincere welcome and declare the official opening of this conference, and on behalf of the government and people of our country, I wish your association great and glorious success."

▲ Minister Huang's Speech "Distinguished Delegates and Members, today is the official opening of the Ninth Conference of your Association. As the honorary vice president of the conference, I am deeply honored to extend my welcome to all of you. The gentlemen present here today are all medical and health experts from various Far Eastern countries. Their usual duties are extremely heavy. This time, they have been able to sacrifice their precious time and travel from thousands of miles away to attend the meeting. This kind of enthusiasm and perseverance can be said to be a spirit of promoting science and a spirit of benevolence and saving the world, which is very admirable. At the same time, in my position as Minister of Interior, I would like to express some opinions on the scope of internal affairs. There are many things included in the scope of internal affairs, but medical and health administration is a very important facility, especially during the construction period. No matter what kind of construction, such as water conservancy, land, rural areas, industry, and transportation, it is closely related to health. It can be said that when various constructions begin, health construction must also be carried out at the same time. Since the establishment of the National Government of our country, great attention has been paid to medical and health construction. First, a Health Department was established in the Ministry of Interior, then a Ministry of Health was established, and then it was changed to a Health Department. Recently, in order to promote health technology and adopt the facilities of emerging countries, a Health Experiment Office was established under the National Economic Commission, so that both administrative and technical parties can plan for development and advance in separate ways. Affiliated agencies are also increasing year by year. In various localities, there are also various health experiment zones in cities, counties, and rural areas. The National Government, in order to further promote the progress of medical and health affairs and international cooperation in the academic community, invited your association to hold the Ninth Conference in the capital of our country four years ago. It is being held at a time when our country is actively engaged in construction, and its benefits are extensive. The medical and health profession has a direct relationship with the lives of the people, so its responsibility is very heavy. Moreover, as world transportation becomes increasingly advanced, the spread of diseases is also becoming easier. The health facilities of one country can affect other countries, so international medical and health cooperation is a very necessary undertaking. The progress and discoveries in the various specialized knowledge discussed by the gentlemen present here today will have an impact on the whole world. I am deeply convinced that scholars and people from all over the world are paying close attention, looking forward to it, and welcoming it. Finally, I sincerely welcome the great success of the conference."

▲ Liu Jui-heng's Opening Address Dr. Liu Jui-heng, Director of the Ministry of Health of China and Chairman of the Conference, said in his opening address, "Today, with the progress of culture, medical and pharmaceutical science is also gradually improving. Therefore, today's medical and pharmaceutical undertakings are very different from those of a hundred or fifty years ago. The most important difference is the application and implementation of new sciences such as preventive medicine, personal hygiene, and public health. If we only use modern treatment methods to treat diseases, medical and pharmaceutical science will certainly not have the progress it has today. A large part of today's medical and pharmaceutical undertakings is indeed aimed at treatment, and it may be like this in the next few years. However, with the progress of culture, methods for preventing diseases are being gradually discovered, making various diseases increasingly preventable, or even making many diseases disappear completely. Looking around, the progress of medical and pharmaceutical undertakings in various countries is not consistent, and even within one country, the progress of facilities in various places is not the same, which is regrettable. Because most places do not have sufficient health protection and various medical and pharmaceutical facilities, and even some areas lack modern doctors and hospitals. This is the case in most Far Eastern countries. Therefore, diseases that can be completely prevented are still prevalent. If all countries can make use of modern knowledge of disease prevention, environmental hygiene, and public health, then the following diseases, such as cholera, smallpox, typhus, typhoid fever, bubonic plague, and leprosy, should be completely eliminated from the ground. The reason why these diseases still exist is that although governments are willing to do their best to protect the people, they have not seen results due to insufficient equipment. If they want to provide the necessary protection, the government should first have sufficient specialized personnel, agencies, and funds. This specialized personnel includes doctors, nurses, pharmacists, dentists, midwives, sanitary engineers, health inspectors, and publicity personnel. The agencies include hospitals, especially isolation hospitals, maternity hospitals, sanatoriums, clinical laboratories, seaport quarantine stations, health centers, and rural health clinics and pharmacies to meet the needs. However, it is not easy to achieve these facilities in a short period of time. All of you present here know that we have a very heavy responsibility. We must raise funds for the construction of agencies and the training of personnel. If we have completed the above three points to a considerable extent, then we can talk about public health undertakings. In my capacity as Director of the Ministry of Health and Director of the Health Experiment Office of the Republic of China, I would like to briefly report to you on the health facilities and work in our country in recent years. I must admit that the various works of prevention and treatment of diseases that our country is currently implementing are still far from the standard. We can be proud of the famous internal and surgical physicians we had thousands of years ago, but since medicine has progressed from the philosophical period to the scientific period, our progress has been very slow. Previous Chinese governments neglected to make full use of modern inventions and discoveries in science, and modern medicine and public health undertakings were rarely implemented in the country. Other scientific products, such as railways, automobiles, radios, and various new-style machines, were imported into China relatively late, and medical science was no exception. Since the overthrow of the former Qing government, various political changes have occurred in the country. Until recently, there was no overall plan for construction in the country. Even now, various progress has not been as we hoped. Many people have asked me why this conference was not held in Shanghai or Beijing. Shanghai is very convenient for hotels, transportation, and other facilities. Beijing has the highest institutions of learning and famous scenic spots such as the Forbidden City, which is also very suitable. However, the government finally chose Nanjing, with the intention of allowing the delegates to observe the new construction undertakings of the Chinese government. Just in terms of health agencies, when the former government was in Beijing, there were only two central epidemic prevention offices, the Northeast Epidemic Prevention Office. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing in 1927, the central health agencies established successively are as follows: Ministry of Health of the Ministry of Interior, Health Experiment Office of the National Economic Commission, National Seaport Quarantine Office, Central Health Testing Institute, Beiping First Midwifery School, Central Hospital, Central Midwifery School, Central Nursing School. At a time when the world is in turmoil, the National Government has been able to create various facilities to meet the needs. In the agenda of this conference, we have arranged for you to visit various agencies. Please pay special attention to the Health Experiment Office and the work of its nine departments. The details have been introduced in the "First Report of the Central Health Experiment Office" and "Image Album of the General Situation of Central Health Facilities" that have been distributed to you. The content is very clear. This place is the center of health experiments and future national health implementation work in China. When the Health Experiment Office was established, it sought various technical opinions from the Health Group of the League of Nations to ensure that its work was in line with the latest standards in various regions. In this short period of three years, there has been considerable progress in the above-mentioned aspects. The most rapid progress has been in the management and prevention of infectious diseases, health education, school health, maternal and child health, medical relief facilities, and the establishment of rural health centers. The most fundamental to the country should be the various training classes held, which have trained various specialized and technical personnel, no less than a public health specialist college, so that health administrators and personnel engaged in bacteriology, parasitology, school health, etc. have the opportunity to study and improve their skills. In addition to the various health agencies established by the central government, there are also considerable new measures for medical and health work in various provinces and major cities. Health agencies such as health experiment offices, health centers, midwifery schools, hospitals, and clinics have been established in various places one after another, and are progressing rapidly. We often encounter difficulties in the above-mentioned works. The vast land, the large population, the old customs and various superstitions of the people, and economic difficulties are all major reasons for hindering the progress of medical construction. However, we have been pioneers in this work. There are now twenty-four medical schools in the country, more than six thousand registered doctors, and hundreds of public and private hospitals, which are powerful forces for protecting the health of the people. We should be optimistic about the future construction. Now, let me say a few more words about this conference. This conference has a history of twenty-six years. In Article 2 of the Association's Constitution and the purpose of the conference, "to make medical personnel in the Far East a close group," and Article 4, "to promote friendship among scientific personnel internationally," the main points of this conference are still the same meaning as the above two points. In fact, our difficulties are the same. The deeper our mutual relationship, the greater our harmony. Furthermore, in the past few months, China has sent several hospital teachers to Little Luzon, Annam, India, Singapore, and the Dutch East Indies to study bovine plague, kala-azar, malaria, etc. They reported after returning to China that they were warmly welcomed in every country they visited and gained many benefits in knowledge. From this, we can see that the relationship between each other is extremely close. The League of Nations and the Rockefeller Foundation Committee have made great contributions to promoting friendship by sending health personnel from various countries to investigate and study. Now is the time when medical personnel in the Far East should be united. I still remember when cholera was epidemic in Shanghai in 1930, after I convened the first cholera prevention meeting, the health leaders of the three public agencies in Shanghai, the Public Concession, the French Concession, and the Shanghai Municipality, cooperated with each other, and I was fortunate to see it. The work of the Oriental Affairs Bureau of the International Federation in contacting seaport quarantine in various countries is also sufficient to show the spirit of international cooperation. I would now like to further suggest to this conference that the work of this conference should pay special attention to international cooperation. Finally, I thank you for electing me as the chairman of this conference and formally express my gratitude for being the host of the Ninth Conference. The conference has just begun, and I firmly believe that in addition to fully achieving the purpose of the conference, it will also enable the Far Eastern countries, especially China, to obtain permanent benefits in terms of medical progress."

He Yingqin's Tour of Chahar and Suiyuan

Inspecting Mongolian Customs and Traditions; Stability in the Provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan 95

(Beiping Correspondence) Since assuming his post in Beiping, Chairman He Yingqin of the Beiping Military Branch has remained in the city for over a year. Aside from a brief trip to Tianjin last winter to visit old friends, he had not left Beiping. Recently, with the clear skies and pleasant weather, and the scenic beauty beyond the Great Wall beckoning, he departed Beiping by special train at 7:00 AM on the 26th of last month for a tour of Chahar and Suiyuan. The public, not knowing the true nature of the trip, engaged in much speculation. Mr. He returned to Beiping at 6:30 PM this afternoon (2nd) and gave a press conference, detailing his travels. The details are as follows:

(Traveling Companions) Those who accompanied Mr. He on this trip included: He Jingwu, member of the Military Branch; Wang Lun, Director; Xie Zhongyuan, Xu Xilin, and Zhang Guanting, Chiefs of Sections; Wang Shanten, Senior Staff Officer; He Chaozhong, Counselor; Lin Qizhi, Secretary; Zhou Yingfang, Aide-de-Camp; and a squad of guards. Shen Chang, Director of the Ping Sui Railway Bureau, also traveled along to ensure smooth arrangements en route.

(Itinerary) Mr. He departed at 7:00 AM on the 26th of last month and arrived in Zhangjiakou at 3:00 PM that afternoon. In addition to attending a banquet hosted by the entire Chahar Provincial Government and attending a welcome reception by various sectors, he spent the night in his special train. On the morning of the 27th, he was guided by Qin Dechun, Director of the Chahar Civil Affairs Department, to inspect the Zhangbei area. He returned to Zhangjiakou that evening and continued his journey by train. On the 28th, he toured the Yungang Grottoes in Datong and spent the night in Zhuozishan. He arrived in Suiyuan at around 7:00 AM on the 29th. Zhao Chengzhou, commander of the Jin Army cavalry stationed in Datong, accompanied him. After arriving in Suiyuan, he visited temples such as the Sheritu Zhao, Wu Pei Temple Zhao, and Chongfu Temple Zhao. He attended a luncheon hosted by Chairman Fu Zuoyi. At 2:00 PM, he reviewed the troops, and at 4:00 PM, he was accompanied by Fu Zuoyi to Baotou. Yesterday (1st), he visited the Kundulun Zhao, accompanied by Fu Zuoyi, Zhao Chengzhou, and Wang Jingguo, commander of the 10th Division stationed in Baotou. He returned to Baotou that day and took the original special train eastward. At 10:30 PM, he passed through Beiping and transferred to the Ping Han Line to Xiling. He arrived at 10:00 AM this morning (2nd), toured for several hours, and returned to Beiping by the original train, disembarking at the West Station at 6:30 PM in the afternoon.

(Rumors Quelled) When Chairman He Yingqin's special train passed through Beiping last night (1st), it only made a brief stop at Guang'anmen Station. Acting Chairman Shang Zhen, Member Wan Fulin, and senior officials of the Military Branch were already waiting at the station to greet him. Security was tight around the station. After Mr. He briefly spoke with Shang Zhen, Wan Fulin, and others in the train, the train departed. At that time, those with oversensitive nerves speculated wildly. With Mr. He's return to Beiping this evening (2nd), all rumors have been dispelled, and the public feels greatly relieved.

(Mr. He's Remarks) After arriving in Beiping this evening (2nd), Mr. He made the following remarks to reporters: "I was appointed to oversee military affairs in Beiping for a year and seven months. During this time, I have not left Beiping once, except for a three-day trip to Tianjin to visit friends. Recently, with the overall situation stable and official duties somewhat lighter, I took the opportunity to travel to Chahar and Suiyuan for a week, reaching Zhangbei in the north and Baotou in the west. I also went from Baotou to the Kundulun Zhao Lama Temple to observe the Mongolian customs and traditions. This trip was purely recreational in nature and had no particular significance. However, due to the convenience of travel, I was able to meet with military and political leaders and local figures along the Ping Sui Railway, and I was deeply impressed by what I saw and heard. My first good impression was that under the governance of Chairmen Song and Fu, the provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan are stable and progressing in construction, showing a vigorous upward trend. Chahar, after the turmoil of several incidents last year, has, in less than a year, eliminated all marauding soldiers and bandits. The towns are clean, and the roads are wide and solid. In the past year, the population of Zhangjiakou has increased from over 60,000 to 90,000, and the population of Zhangbei County has increased from 3,000 to over 10,000. If this continues, the future prospects are bright. Chairman Fu Zuoyi of Suiyuan governs the army and people with a practical and responsible approach. Major policies such as digging canals, promoting land reclamation and animal husbandry, and improving sheep breeds have been deeply rooted, which is truly admirable. Today, those who discuss national affairs and policies all advocate for the development of the Northwest. The Northwest is vast and sparsely populated. There are not enough people to fully utilize its resources. For example, Suiyuan has an area of 1.2 million square li, but a population of only 2.5 million, with only two people per square li, which is a stark contrast to the densely populated provinces in the interior. In the future, immigration to populate the border regions is a fundamental solution, both for resolving livelihood issues and strengthening national power. Furthermore, the reason why the provinces of Chahar and Suiyuan have been able to move towards construction is primarily due to the blessing of peace and secondly, due to the ethical efforts of the responsible authorities. Peace is the prerequisite for construction, and ethical effort is the foundation of construction. Only with peace can we devote ourselves to construction, and only with ethical effort can we be clean and efficient, and can we rationalize construction. Extending this from Chahar and Suiyuan to the entire North China region, from a military perspective alone, I was appointed during a time of crisis and have勉维 the status quo. There is nothing to speak of in terms of achievements. The most important thing today is to revitalize the spirit of the people, promote traditional morality, maintain credibility and harmony externally within a reasonable scope, and have the awareness of self-reliance and self-help internally. With this great awareness, we can truly transform North China. This requires the guidance of the central government, the cooperation of local political and military authorities, and the unity of the people's organizations. With concerted efforts, we must work hard. This is not a task that can be accomplished by one person or in a short period of time. We can only redouble our reflection and effort." (2nd)

Yangtze River National Products Tour (Continued) Heng. 96

Wuhu is an important port along the Yangtze River, with a population of 180,000. Since opening to trade, its commerce has gradually developed, becoming a major rice market in Anhui Province. The commercial situation was very prosperous before the 20th year of the Republic (1931). However, the great flood of that year caused the streets to be several feet deep in water, which persisted for a long time, leading to a significant decline in the market that has not yet recovered. The city has six banks, ten money shops, twelve large silk and cloth stores, five large hardware stores, and twenty-five large rice shops. There is one yarn factory, Yuzhong, two soap factories, five machine factories, and the Mingda Electric Light Company. There are four middle schools for boys, two middle schools for girls, and two vocational schools. Foreign firms include Jardine Matheson, Swire, Nisshin, Asiatic Petroleum, Socony, and Texaco. In terms of finance, bank deposits have increased, while money shops have declined. Few stores have strong financial backing, and it is difficult to maintain business in the current economic downturn. In addition to daily steamboat services on the Yangtze River, Wuhu has the Jing-Wu Road and the Wu-Tun Road, which is a major artery in southern Anhui. The southern section of the Zha-Wu Railway has been opened to Xuancheng, and the northern section is planned to connect with the Jing-Hu (Nanjing-Shanghai) Railway, which will further develop business. It is generally observed that the Wuhu market is built on the rice market. It produces 12 million shi of rice annually. In the future, if a railway is built in northern Anhui, connecting Huaiyuan to Yuxi on the opposite bank of Wuhu, where it would connect with the Zha-Wu Road, the Wuhu market will have even greater prospects.

To understand the industrial and commercial situation of Wuhu, one can find some information from the Customs Report. The following are the import and export statistics for Wuhu in the 20th year of the Republic (1931) (due to lack of recent Customs Reports):

Value of Imported Foreign Goods (Customs Taels)

Foreign Cloths: 1,944,673

Woolens: 73,701

Electrical Materials: 88,798

Coal: 76,560

Paper: 152,841

Dyes: 237,977

Cigarettes: 504,185

Sugar: 1,577,396

Wheat: 32,890

Hardware: 405,702

Other: 4,190,075

Total: 9,303,798

Value of Exported Local Goods (to Overseas and Domestic Ports)

Rice: 19,409,976

Grains: 26,557

Tea: 0,709

Peanuts: 36,120

Flour: 84,967

Cotton: 358,050

Wheat: 16,083

Beans: 56,185

Fresh Products: 1,544,731

Other: 791,216

Total: 22,336,594

From the above table, it can be seen that Wuhu is centered on agricultural products, and imported goods are mainly clothing materials, which is worthy of our attention. Comparing exports and imports, there is a surplus of over 13 million taels, which is naturally offset by domestic goods. Overland transportation is not included. Local administrations are striving to propose and build roads. If roads are built in all directions, Wuhu City will be the central hub for the transport of agricultural products from the Yangtze River.

(Jiading)

Jiading, Taicang, Baoshan Telephone Service 97

Jiading, Taicang, and Baoshan counties are adjacent to each other. For the purpose of liaison and defense, the county governments of the three counties have already connected telephone lines, but they were limited to official use. From October 1st, private users will also be able to make calls. Regardless of whether the call is to Taicang or Baoshan, the charge is one dime per call. However, users must first deposit a registration fee of five yuan at the telephone bureau.

(Songjiang)

Registration Status of Opium Smokers in This County 98

The registration of opium smokers in this county has been extended repeatedly, and will end on September 30th, without any further extensions. The Anti-Opium Committee has issued instructions to all districts and announcements to all sectors of society. The County Anti-Opium Committee dispatched personnel to various districts to issue licenses. These included Wang Bangzhen in the first district (urban area), Feng Keren in the second district (Sijing), Zheng Xiuzhi in the third district (Xinzhuang), Zha Zizhi in the fourth district (Tianmashan), Lu Zimo in the fifth district (Fengjing), Wu Guangbiao in the sixth district (Yexie), Wang Jicai in the seventh district (Tinglin), and Li Wenxue in the eighth district (Shanyang). They departed on the 25th and ended on the 30th. The districts are currently compiling the results, which have not yet been verified. Currently, the first district (urban area) has issued 324 Class A licenses and 970 Class B licenses, which is significantly different from the original reported registration. This is likely due to a lack of understanding in the rural areas and a wait-and-see attitude. It is reported that some people are planning to request the County Anti-Opium Committee to allow a ten-day extension, citing the example of Jiangning County. It is said that if there are only over 1,200 opium smokers in the urban area, which is less than 40-50% of the actual number, then an extension is essential.

(Suzhou)

Surveying the Disaster Situation in the Entire County 99

Due to the drought this year, the harvests in the rural areas of Wu County have been greatly reduced. According to the reports of crop failure from farmers in various villages, the yield is estimated to be just over 50%. Landowners have now organized a Disaster Survey Committee and have scheduled for tomorrow (5th) to dispatch a large number of surveyors, divided into thirteen groups, to conduct on-site surveys in various villages. The total survey expenses are estimated to be over 11,000 yuan. The county government has approved an allocation of 1,700 yuan in silver from local funds, with the remainder to be borne by the landowners. The committee has also requested the county government to allocate an additional 3,000 yuan.

Businesses Refuse to Pay Security Expenses 100

The security expenses for the Wu County Security Corps have been collected under the house tax. Since the Security Corps was reorganized into the Security Brigade last month and placed under the command of the Provincial Security Office, the business community has requested the county government to cancel the collection of security expenses to reduce the burden on merchants. The county government did not approve this request. Recently, when personnel from the local tax collection office went to collect the taxes, businesses refused to pay. The County Magistrate of Wu believes that this matter has greatly affected the regular tax revenue and issued an order yesterday (3rd) to the County Chamber of Commerce, instructing all businesses to pay in full to maintain tax revenue.

(Wuxi)

Improvement Fees to be Collected for Spring Cocoons Sold in Autumn 101

The silkworm and jujube model area in this county is implementing a cocoon bank system in the province, and improvement fees are being collected for dried cocoons. However, there is no standard for the collection of fees for spring cocoons sold in autumn. Therefore, a request was submitted to the province for instructions. Yesterday, instructions were received stating that the improvement fees for spring cocoons sold in autumn should also be collected at the autumn rate of six yuan per dan. As for the scarcity of cocoon banks open for business during this season, which is insufficient to purchase fresh cocoons, a joint office for the cooperative production and sales of the sericulture industry should be established to handle the cooperative production and sales of dried cocoons to provide relief.

Yixing Drought Relief Group Comes to Wuxi 102

Yixing is located between the three major watersheds of the Tao Lake, Ge Lake, and Tai Lake, and is known as a water town. Therefore, it has historically suffered from frequent floods. This year, however, it has been plagued by a severe drought with no rain. Initially, efforts were made to bail water, but eventually the rivers and canals dried up, making it impossible to save the crops. Eight hundred thousand mu of farmland in the county have been affected, accounting for about eight-tenths of the county's total farmland. All crops have been lost. The severity of the disaster is no less than that of Liyang. Recently, the county organized a Drought Relief Committee and appointed Yang Chu, Zhu Zhongjing, and Yu Xunlu as representatives to come to Wuxi yesterday to contact the Chamber of Commerce and the Red Swastika Society to discuss relief efforts. Lu Bohong, a philanthropist from Shanghai, also came to Wuxi yesterday to meet with Cai Jiansan, president of the Wuxi Red Swastika Society, to inspect the disaster situation in Yixing and Liyang counties and prepare to raise funds for disaster relief.

Continuous Rain Delays Early Rice Harvest 103

This county experienced a severe drought for two months this summer, causing a disaster. The rice in various villages had a glimmer of hope due to the efforts to bail water. However, just as the early rice harvest was about to begin, continuous rain suddenly fell, preventing the harvest. If the rain continues, the rice stalks will inevitably rot, greatly reducing the harvest. Farmers, who were waiting for the new rice to cook, are suffering greatly from this delay.

(Changzhou)

Villager Murder Case Solved, Culprit Arrested 104

Chen Xikun, a villager from Hanshu Village in the fourth district of Wu County, was murdered while guarding his rice field. The Anjiasha Police Station arrested a suspect, Chen Xipang, because he had a lot of blood on his head and other parts of his body. After questioning, the suspect confessed that the main culprits were Jiang Rongxing, Gao Jinyu, and others. The police station immediately dispatched officers to arrest Jiang Rongxing. Gao Jinyu escaped, and his brother, Gao Erbao, was brought to the station. The other suspects have all fled. Guan Junjie, a prosecutor from the County Court, went to the village on the morning of the 2nd to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy revealed multiple knife wounds on the head and chest, confirming that the victim had been repeatedly stabbed to death while alive. After the autopsy, the culprits Chen Loupang and Jiang Rongxing, as well as the suspect Gao Erbao, were brought from the Anjiasha Police Station to the city to be interrogated according to the law. The motive for the murder was the failure to borrow a water buffalo.

(Jiangyin)

Soldiers Causing Trouble on the Zhencheng Road, Provincial Security Office Strictly Investigating 105

On September 11th, guards on the Zhencheng Road (Zhenjiang-Chengdu) Chengwu section, soldiers from the 3rd Battalion of the 3rd Regiment of the Provincial Security Corps, clashed with road workers, shooting and injuring several workers, killing one worker, Zhao Zhengcai. After County Magistrate Bao reported this incident to the provincial government, Wan Xicui Fang from Wujin also requested the Provincial Security Office to investigate. Director Xiang ordered the County Magistrate of Wujin to respond and, together with the Civil Affairs and Construction Departments, ordered the commander of the 3rd Regiment of the Security Corps to strictly investigate the soldiers who caused the trouble.

Qingyang Farmers Block Cars 106

The Xicheng (Wuxi-Jiangyin) long-distance bus hit and injured a villager, Zhao Aqi, near the Qingyang station the other day and was sent to Jiangyin Hospital for treatment. The villagers believed that the car accident involved human life and gathered hundreds of farmers on the morning of the 1st to lie on the road, preventing the long-distance bus from passing. The Qingyang branch station reported to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Patrol Officer Yang Qu went to persuade them for a long time, but to no avail. At that time, many cars were blocked. Liu, Director of the Telephone Bureau, sent Zhang Patrol Officer and police to persuade them earnestly. The farmers gradually dispersed.

(Haimen)

Jinghai Warship Sailed to Shanghai for Repairs 107

The Jinghai warship of this county has not been repaired for a long time, the paint has peeled off, and the equipment is decayed and rusted. After submitting a request to the county government and approving a budget of 1,000 yuan, it sailed to Shanghai the other day to enter the factory for repairs. All the soldiers, led by Cannon Chief Zhou Youqi, rented civilian houses in Qinglonggang for temporary residence. The ship's repair time is expected to be about one month.

(Zhenjiang)

Anti-Opium Association Strictly Arrests Those Concealing Opium 108

The Zhenjiang County Anti-Opium Committee stated that the registration of opium smokers ended on September 30th. Although the total number of registrations has not yet been fully reported, it is inevitable that some people will attempt to conceal opium and avoid court appearances. In order to strictly enforce the anti-opium policy, in addition to ordering the subordinate investigators to conduct thorough investigations, the Provincial Public Security Bureau was specifically requested to conduct a detailed investigation and strictly arrest those who conceal opium in the urban area. Regarding the rural areas, a conference of district chiefs was convened to discuss methods and conduct thorough investigations in the countryside in order to emphasize the anti-opium policy and avoid concealment.

Fireworks Display at the Commodities Exhibition 109

The Provincial Commodities Exhibition officially opened on the first of this month. There have been many visitors in recent days. In order to arouse public interest, the association sent a commissioner to Jiangdu to order exquisite fireworks, which are scheduled to be set off at the Provincial Public Stadium on the evening of Double Ten Festival (October 10th). Gou Zengji, director of the Nantong Land Tax Bureau, has been found guilty of land tax fraud. Ye Pengchun from the Provincial Committee has arrived in Nantong to thoroughly investigate. Gou's land and property have been seized by the county government as collateral.

(Jiaxing)

Date Set for Sentencing in Agricultural Bank Embezzlement Case 113

The major theft and embezzlement case at the Jiaxing Farmers Bank has been tried several times, and all those involved have been detained. On the 2nd, the court held another hearing. The defense lawyers for the defendants also appeared in court. The judge, Zhou Ding, summoned the defendants Xu Fukang, Tu Yiran, Tu Haigen, Jiang Shiyuan, Tu Amao, Zhi Asi, Feng Xingsun, Chen Afa, and Li Jinbao, as well as the witnesses Wu Jinpu and Chen Xu, for questioning one by one. Their testimonies were the same as in the previous court. Finally, the defense lawyers Jiang Weixian, Ren Jiaju, and Gao Jian, etc., made their respective defenses and requested that Xu Fukang and Tu Yiran be released on bail, which was not approved. Wu Yunbin, the lawyer representing the Agricultural Bank in the incidental civil suit, requested that the defendants be ordered to jointly compensate the Agricultural Bank for the confirmed loss of 43,361.46 yuan (the rural loans are still under investigation). Judge Zhou announced the conclusion of the debate in court and set the date for sentencing on the 8th. Xu Fukang, Tu Yiran, and the other five people were still taken into custody, while Feng Xingsun, Chen Afa, and Li Jinbao were released on their original bail. The rest were ordered to return.

Number of Councilors in Each District Determined 114

The number of councilors in Jiaxing County has been determined according to the number of citizens in each district. District 1 should elect three people, District 2 should elect one person, Districts 3, 4, 5, and 6 should each elect two people, and District 7 should elect three people. The township and town offices are currently compiling the citizen registers to be submitted to the district offices for consolidation and then to the county government for verification.

Two Pawnshops Announce Suspension of Pawning 115

The Ziyuan, Hengyuan, and Juyuan money shops in the North City of Jiaxing, due to the impact of deposit withdrawals by various depositors, had difficulty in circulation and announced the suspension of business on September 30th. They are currently clearing their accounts. After the three shops closed down, businesses related to the shareholders of the shops (the Cheng family) were also affected. The first to be affected were the Dachang pawnshop on Zhong Street and the Renxin pawnshop in Wangdian. Due to the difficulty in allocating working capital and the hopelessness of obtaining funds, they announced the suspension of pawning and waiting for redemption from the 3rd, which has been reported to the county for record. Such a phenomenon will make the poor people even more terrified.

(Jintan)

Investigation of the Disaster Situation in Each District 117

The drought this year in Tanyi (Jintan County) is extremely severe. Not only have the high-lying areas been unable to plant crops, but also the low-lying areas near the lake have become barren due to the drying up of the lake. According to the investigation, the areas with the most severe disaster in the county are: the first district, the area near the city; the second district, Hetou, Yaotang, Zhongtang, and other places; the third district, Xiaoqiu, Antou, and other places; the fourth district, Zhiqian, Biao She, Tou Dong Pu, and other places; the fifth district, Xuebu, Tangwang, Luocun, Bahekou Tushan, and other places; and the sixth district, Xiyang, Shimaqiao, and other places. It is estimated that 600,000 to 700,000 mu of farmland in the county have been affected, and there are 150,000 to 160,000 disaster victims, making it the worst drought in nearly a century.

(Yangzhou)

Heavy Rain in Huai Area, Canal Water Rises 118

Due to heavy rains in various counties of the Huai area lasting for a day and a night, the water level of the canal rose. The Liutang River and Hongze Lake also flooded into the central canal, making it difficult to discharge the water. From the 1st, the water level suddenly rose downstream of Gao Bao, with waves rolling and rushing like arrows. Fortunately, the Canal Works Bureau had made thorough preparations in advance along the canal banks, and there was no impact. However, continuous rain has been falling since the 2nd, and the weather has suddenly turned cold like that of the Double Ninth Festival. If it does not clear up, the canal water will continue to rise.

(Qingjiang)

Heat Wave and Hurricane Strike Huaiyin 119

In the Huaiyin County area, the weather suddenly turned hot again starting on the 28th of last month, unlike the climate of autumn. On the 29th, the temperature reached as high as 95 degrees Fahrenheit, which was unprecedented. Suddenly, after 8:00 PM last night (30th), the weather changed dramatically. A strong wind blew, mixed with light rain, which did not stop all night. Although the wind has subsided this morning, when the wind was extremely strong last night, 20-30 thatched houses in the countryside were blown away. Many newly harvested bean stalks that had not been piled up properly in the countryside were also blown down. However, due to the lack of heavy rain, there have been no reports of broken wires or fallen trees on telegraph and telephone poles.

(Xiaoshan)

Two Children Arguing Over Watching a Play Leads to Murder 120

At the Guangyutang in Changhe Town, Xiaoshan, there was a play being performed on the night of the 30th. Lai Yousheng's son, Shou Rong (13 years old), and Tang Azheng's son, Tang Shunkang (15 years old), had an argument over seating. They then fought with their bare hands. Subsequently, Lai's son stabbed Tang's son in the chest with a small foreign knife. Shunkang immediately collapsed to the ground in extreme pain and died after a while. The Tang family immediately reported to the local police station and the County Court. Prosecutor Zheng and Inspector Zhao rushed to the scene in Changhe to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy revealed a knife wound on the chest of the deceased, confirming that he died as a result of the injury. Shou Rong, the murderer, and his father, Yousheng, were immediately taken to the county for detention, pending prosecution and investigation.

(Ningbo)

New Jail of Local Court Completed 121

The construction of the new jail of the Yinxian Local Court, which was jointly funded by all sectors of Ningbo, began on January 25th of this year. After eight months of construction and an expenditure of 70,000 yuan, the entire project was completed on the 10th of last month. The jail was opened for one day yesterday (1st), and two to three thousand leaders and people from all walks of life in this port went to the scene to visit. The buildings of the jail were built on the original site of the old elementary school, covering an area of about two mu. The form is a two-story T-shaped Western-style building. In addition to offices, bathrooms, and interview rooms, there are 49 men's cells, 5 women's cells, and 6 civil affairs custody cells. Each cell can accommodate ten people. The internal equipment is quite complete. It is not yet determined when the current inmates will be transferred.

Appointment of Envoy to Italy to be Elevated and Announced Next Week

Proposed Appointment of Minister Liu Wentao as Ambassador to Italy Will Be Announced Soon, To Enter Beijing to Receive Instructions 122

According to the Central News Agency, the elevation of our country's legation in Italy to an embassy has been approved by the 180th Executive Yuan meeting. Anqin Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Will Take a Ship to Hong Kong on the 9th, Transferring to India and Entering Tibet 123

Pujing Lama Anqin Khutuktu arrived in Shanghai at 2:30 PM yesterday by the Beijing-Zhabei express train from Beijing and is staying at the Winsome Hotel. According to him, this trip to Tibet is to arrange for the return of the Panchen Lama to Tibet and has no other mission. He has decided to take the Italian ship Conte Verde to Hong Kong on the 9th, transfer to India, and enter Tibet. Buddhist groups in the city plan to request him to preach for three days. The details are as follows:

Arrival Situation Those who went to the North Station to welcome him yesterday included Wang Zhinan, representative of Yang Hu, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau; Li Jingyu, Director of the Panchen Lama's Shanghai Office; representatives of Buddhist groups such as the Chinese Buddhist Association, the Buddhist Pure Land Society, and the Esoteric Buddhist Abode; Master Bao; and lay Buddhists Zhao Yiwu and Qu Wenliu.

Anqin Living Buddha (Photo by Qichang) 124

More than 20 people were present. The Security Bureau also sent two squads of soldiers to maintain strict guard around the station and on the platform. After Anqin Lama got off the train and took a photo, he immediately took a car to the Winsome Hotel on Route Lafayette to rest. The people who came with him included Secretary-General Wang Luojie, the chanting Khenpo, and 32 attendants. The Lama is staying in Room 5 on the second floor of the hotel, while the attendants are staying in separate rooms.

Statement Upon arriving at his residence, the Lama spoke with Master Bao and representatives of Buddhist groups. The Lama was wearing a yellow robe and a melon-style hat with a red topknot, and deep yellow monk shoes. Although his hair was graying, he was energetic and amiable. When meeting with reporters, he stated through a translator that this trip to Tibet was entirely to arrange for the return of the Panchen Lama to Tibet, as the Lama is scheduled to depart next spring. He himself plans to leave Shanghai on the 9th of this month on the Italian postal company's Conte Verde, arrive in Hong Kong, transfer to another ship, and enter Tibet via Calcutta, India. He does not intend to delay in India. After arriving in Tibet, he will meet with Huang, the special envoy (Mu Song), but the central government has not given him any documents to convey. Once arrangements are made in Tibet, he plans to return to Nanjing as soon as possible. Those accompanying him to Tibet include Secretary-General Wang Luojie, the chanting Khenpo, and 30 attendants. He will do his best to promote the central government's goodwill during this trip to Tibet.

Request to Preach Local Buddhist groups, such as the Buddhist Pure Land Society, believe that the Lama's transit through Shanghai on this trip to Tibet is a rare opportunity and have initiated a public invitation to the Lama to preach at the Jueyuan Temple on Hart Road for three days. They also plan to hold a banquet to welcome him at that time. Representatives were sent yesterday to request him in person. It is said that the Lama has agreed, but the date of commencement has not yet been determined.

The President of the Red Cross Society and Others Officially Took Office Yesterday
